 ' iske baad 'big bos' ne rohan kii captaini chin lee or elaan kiya ki puure sijan main ab vah kabhi captain nahin ban paaenge

 unhone is baat par bhi aapatti jataai ki ab unhen dobaaraa captain nahin banaaya jayega

 is bich manu or monalisa agali captaini par baat karte najar aae vahiin swami om ne kaha ki rohan main ghamand aa gaya tha or acha hua ki 'big bos' ne unhen hataa diya

 iske baad manavir, priyanka or manu ne swami om ke gadde or saamaan kii talaashi lee

 mona ne donon kii baat sun lee or unhen peeth peeche manu or manavir kii buraai karne se manaa kiya
 Shortly after this, there was a fierce debate between Priyanka and Monalisa in the kitchen area
 monalisa ne priyanka se kaha ki vah koi nahin hoti unhen unki limits bataane vaali, manu ne bich bachaav kii tab jaakar donon kaa jhagada shant hua
 During this time also, Captain Rohan made no attempt to pacify both
 kuch der baad priyanka mona ko apane paale main karti najar ai

 tab rohan ne kaha ki vah puri koshish kar rahe hai lekin 'big bos' behatar bataa paaenge

 Netaji Subhash Chandra Bose's naib and Pandit Jawaharlal Nehru's 'old friend' ACN Nambiar was a spy of the Soviet Union
 british dastavejon main yah daawa kiya gaya he
 Confidential documents from the UK National Archives have been made public
 unke anusaar nambiar 1924 main ek patrkaar ke rup main berlin gaye the or vahaan bhartiya communist samooh ke saath milakar kaam kiya tha
 He went to Moscow in 1929 as a 'guest' of the Soviet
 dastavejon main kaha gaya he ki dwitiya vishwayuddh shuru hone ke baad nambiar ko germany se nirvasit kar diya gaya, lekin baad main unhen bose ke naayab ke taur par berlin aane kii manjuuri de di gai
 After this, when Bose went from Germany to the Far East to join Japan, Nambiar was given the responsibility of the financial leader (german) of the Azad Hind Fauj in Europe
 abhilekhaagaar kii ore se jari bayaan ke anusaar nambiar bhartiya yudhbandiyon ko milakar bane us bhartiya sainya samooh se bhi sambandhit the jise 1944 main soviet sangh ne apane saath milaayaa tha
 Nambiar was arrested in Austria in June 1945 and the Nazis were interrogated
 dwitiya vishwa yuddh ke baad nambiar switzraland ke bern sthit bhartiya mishan main bataur vaanijya doot tathaa scandinavia main bataur bhartiya rajdoot kaam karne lage or baad main pashchim germany chale
 He then worked as the European correspondent of 'hindustan Times'
 dastavejon main daawa kiya gaya ki nambiar ko audyogic khufia gatividhiyon ko cover karne ke liye tainaat kiya gaya tha
 British documents include names and descriptions of Netaji's activities related to Azad Hind in Europe and Germany
 dastowajon main un patron kii pratiyaan bhi hai jo nambiar ne bose ko likhe the

 aaj madar terresi kii jayanti he

 unka vaastavik naam agness gonjha boyajiju tha
 The Mother Teresakonobel Shanti Award, which laid its life in the service of leprosy patients and orphans, has been awarded
 duniya main or khaas taur se bhartiya upmahadweep main aisa hi koi hoga jo madar terresa ke naam or krity se waakif na ho
 He devoted his entire life to the service of others
 aaj jaanate hai madar terresa ke bare main kuch dilachasp baaten
 
 
 - Mother Teresa Agnesse Gonkshe was a Catholic of Bozshiu, but she was a citizen of India
 unhen bharat ke saath saath kai anya deshon kii naagarikta mili hui thi, jisamen automan, srbija, bulgeria or yugoslavia shaamil he
 In the year 1946, he pledged to serve the poor and helpless
 niswaarth seva ke liye terresa ne 1950 main kolkata main 'mishanrij of cherity' kii sthapana kii thi
 He changed his name in 1981
 - albania mul kii madar terresa ne kolkata main garibon or peedit logon ke liye jo kiya wo duniya main abhootpurv mana jaataa he
 - He started his organization with 12 members and now the organization is operating in 133 countries

 1
 Vivek Oberoi was born on 3 September 1976 in Hyderabad

 Vivek's father is well-known actor Suresh Oberoi and mother Yashodhara Oberoi
 3
 Vivek's full name is 'vivek Anand Oberoi'

 Why is waterproofing necessary? Sanjay, on any construction surface, water causes cracks such as cracks, which can lead to long-term house damage
 isi prakaar, deevaaron par nami mold vruddhi main yogadan detii he, yah un anek kaarnon main se ek he jo asthma jaise shwasan rogon ko janm dete hai

 Where to do waterproofing? Basic waterproofing is done in some new homes, but it is limited to roofs only
 lekin apane ghar ko hyae 5-point li-free home banane ke liye jaruri he ki ghar ke un sabhi hisson main waterprufing karai jaae, jahaan se pani ke ghusane kii ashanka ho

 yah samajhnaa mahatvapurn he ki vibhinn satahon ko vibhinn prakaar kii chunautiyon kaa saamana karnaa padataa he, isliye in satahon main se prayek ko waterpruf banane ke liye apni shrenee ke sarvottam samaadhaan kaa istemaal karnaa chahie
 The house will be fully protected only when proper waterproofing is done in all five possible water logging areas
 ye paanch sataha mahatvapurn hai or iske kuch kaaran hai, jo is prakaar hai-1
 Under the ground - surface water increases over a period of time and can enter your home, damaging the internal walls
 2
 Indoor Wet Areas (bathrooms, kitchens and balconies) - These areas are exposed to water continuously for 365 days, which causes paint on the interior walls to deteriorate and crush
 3
 Roof - Along with the change in temperature, the surface of the roof also changes, causing water to leak on your beautiful roof and this brings moisture to the entire house
 4
 Concrete water tanks - These water tanks cause leakage through the surface due to the formation of cracks
 isliye is kshetra kii sahi dhang se waterprufing karnaa mahatvapurn he
 5
 bahari deevaaren - taapmaana main parivartan ke kaaran bahari deevaaron main daraaren paidaa hone lagati he, jisase nami aane lagati he or isliye aapke ghar kaa luk bhi bigadane lagata he

 ye gaanaa kumaar sanu ne anuraadhaa podwal ke saath gaaya tha
 The magic of Dard karra-kumar Sanu was seen after a long time in Ayushmann Khurrana's film Dum Laga Ke Haisha
 unhone dard karaara song ko gaaya
 The new song of 'detective Byomkesh Bakshi', 'bach Ke Bakshi' has been released
 is gane main sushant hip hop dance karte najar aa rahe hai
 The lyrics of this song are 'bach ke bakshi tu jhootha hai makkar'
 gane ko film ke lead actor sushant rajput par filmaaya gaya he
 In this, the beautiful dancers are seen doing energetic dance moves
 film main byomakesh bakshiper filmaae gaye seens ko is gane main dance kii shakl di gai he
 This is what makes this song special
 gane kii is khaas video ko koreograph kiya he dance koreographer lauren gotalieb ne
 Kodibakar Banerjee, who is going to release on April 3, has directed
